set key top left
set term post enhanced colour
set title "{/Symbol e}_n(x); Laser = %subme3 ps; spot = %subme4 mm; %subme5 nC; \
Gun = %subme6 MV/m, %subme7^o; \n Linac1 = %subme8 MV/m, %subme9^o; \
Buck/sol = %submea T; L1 sol1 = %submeb T; L1 sol2 = %submec T; \n \
S02Q1 = %submef k; S02Q2 = %submeg k; S02Q3 = %submeh k; S02Q4 = %submei k; \n \
C2VQ1 = %submej k; C2VQ2 = %submek k; C2VQ3 = %submel k; \
VELQ1 = %submem k; \n VELQ2 = %submen k; VELQ3 = %submeo k; VELQ4 = %submep k; \
VELQ5 = %submeq k; \n VELQ6 = %submer k; \
BA1Q1 = %submes k; BA1Q2 = %submet k; BA1Q3 = %submeu k; \n BA1Q4 = %submev k; \
BA1Q5 = %submew k; BA1Q6 = %submex k; BA1Q7 = %submey k; \n \
%subme2k MP; sc %submee; msc %submez"
set output 'emitt_%subme1_%sub2_x_2BA1.eps'
set xlabel 'z [m]'
set ylabel '{/Symbol e}_n(x) [mm mrad]'
#set xtics 0.2
set mxtics 5
set mytics 5
plot \
'run%subme1/2BA1_%subme1.Xemit.%subme1' u 1:6 \
t 'Astra run %sub1: %sbsta2 %sbsta3 %sbsta4 %sbsta5 \
%sbsta6 %sbsta7 %sbsta8 %sbsta9 %sbstaa %sbstab \
%sbstac %sbstae %sbstaf %sbstag %sbstah \
%sbstai %sbstaj %sbstak %sbstal %sbstam %sbstan \
%sbstao %sbstap %sbstaq %sbstar %sbstas %sbstat \
%sbstau %sbstav %sbstaw %sbstax %sbstay %sbstaz \
%sub3' w l lw 3, \
      'run%sub2/2BA1_%sub2.Xemit.%sub2' u 1:6 \
t 'Astra run %sub2: %sbstb2 %sbstb3 %sbstb4 %sbstb5 \
%sbstb6 %sbstb7 %sbstb8 %sbstb9 %sbstba %sbstbb \
%sbstbc %sbstbe %sbstbf %sbstbg %sbstbh \
%sbstbi %sbstbj %sbstbk %sbstbl %sbstbm %sbstbn \
%sbstbo %sbstbp %sbstbq %sbstbr %sbstbs %sbstbt \
%sbstbu %sbstbv %sbstbw %sbstbx %sbstby %sbstbz \
%sub4' w l lw 3

set title "x-px(0619); Laser = %subme3 ps; spot = %subme4 mm; %subme5 nC; \
Gun = %subme6 MV/m, %subme7^o; \n Linac1 = %subme8 MV/m, %subme9^o; \
Buck/sol = %submea T; L1 sol1 = %submeb T; L1 sol2 = %submec T; \n \

%subme2k MP; sc %submee; msc %submez"
set output 'phase_%subme1_%sub2_x_px_0619_BA1.eps'

#set xtics 2
#set ytics 1.5

'run%subme1/BA1.ren_%subme1.0619.%subme1' u 1:4 \
